file_path="artifact_generation_system.py">\n"""\nArtifact Generation System\nGenerates various types of artifacts from solidified living documents\n"""\n\nimport json\nimport uuid\nfrom datetime import datetime\nfrom typing import Dict, List, Optional, Any\nfrom enum import Enum\nimport asyncio\n\nclass ArtifactType(Enum):\n    """Types of artifacts that can be generated"""\n    PDF = "pdf"\n    DOCX = "docx"\n    CODE = "code"\n    DESIGN = "design"\n    DATA = "data"\n    REPORT = "report"\n    PRESENTATION = "presentation"\n    CONTRACT = "contract"\n\nclass ArtifactStatus(Enum):\n    """Status of artifact generation"""\n    PENDING = "pending"\n    GENERATING = "generating"\n    VALIDATING = "validating"\n    COMPLETE = "complete"\n    FAILED = "failed"\n\nclass Artifact:\n    """Represents a generated artifact"""\n    \n    def __init__(self, artifact_type: ArtifactType, name: str, source_doc_id: str):\n        self.id = str(uuid.uuid4())\n        self.type = artifact_type\n        self.name = name\n        self.source_doc_id = source_doc_id\n        self.status = ArtifactStatus.PENDING\n        self.content = None\n        self.metadata = {}\n        self.version = 1\n        self.versions = []\n        self.quality_score = 0.0\n        self.validation_results = []\n        self.created_at = datetime.now().isoformat()\n        self.updated_at = datetime.now().isoformat()\n        self.file_path = None\n        self.file_size = 0\n        self.format = artifact_type.value\n        \n    def to_dict(self) -> Dict:\n        """Convert artifact to dictionary"""\n        return {\n            \'id\': self.id,\n            \'type\': self.type.value,\n            \'name\': self.name,\n            \'source_doc_id\': self.source_doc_id,\n            \'status\': self.status.value,\n            \'content\': self.content,\n            \'metadata\': self.metadata,\n            \'version\': self.version,\n            \'versions\': self.versions,\n            \'quality_score\': self.quality_score,\n            \'validation_results\': self.validation_results,\n            \'created_at\': self.created_at,\n            \'updated_at\': self.updated_at,\n            \'file_path\': self.file_path,\n            \'file_size\': self.file_size,\n            \'format\': self.format\n        }\n\nclass ArtifactGenerator:\n    """Base class for artifact generators"""\n    \n    def __init__(self, llm_router=None):\n        self.llm_router = llm_router\n        \n    async def generate(self, document: Dict, prompts: List[str], swarm_results: List[Dict]) -> Artifact:\n        """Generate artifact from document, prompts, and swarm results"""\n        raise NotImplementedError("Subclasses must implement generate()")\n        \n    async def validate(self, artifact: Artifact) -> Dict:\n        """Validate generated artifact"""\n        raise NotImplementedError("Subclasses must implement validate()")\n\nclass PDFGenerator(ArtifactGenerator):\n    """Generates PDF documents"""\n    \n    async def generate(self, document: Dict, prompts: List[str], swarm_results: List[Dict]) -> Artifact:\n        """Generate PDF from document"""\n        artifact = Artifact(ArtifactType.PDF, f"{document[\'title\']}.pdf", document[\'id\'])\n        artifact.status = ArtifactStatus.GENERATING\n        \n        # Simulate PDF generation using LLM\n        if self.llm_router:\n            content_prompt = f"""Generate a professional PDF document with the following:\nTitle: {document[\'title\']}\nContent: {document[\'content\']}\nExpertise Level: {document.get(\'expertise_depth\', 0)}\n\nCreate structured sections with:\n- Executive Summary\n- Main Content (organized by sections)\n- Technical Details\n- Conclusions\n- References\n\nFormat as markdown that can be converted to PDF."""\n            \n            response = await self.llm_router.generate(content_prompt, temperature=0.3)\n            artifact.content = response.get(\'content\', \'\')\n        else:\n            # Fallback: structured content\n            artifact.content = f"""# {document[\'title\']}\n\n## Executive Summary\n{document[\'content\'][:200]}...\n\n## Main Content\n{document[\'content\']}\n\n## Technical Details\nExpertise Depth: {document.get(\'expertise_depth\', 0)}\nDomain: {document.get(\'domain_name\', \'General\')}\n\n## Conclusions\nThis document represents a comprehensive analysis of the subject matter.\n\n## References\nGenerated from Living Document ID: {document[\'id\']}\n"""\n        \n        artifact.status = ArtifactStatus.VALIDATING\n        artifact.metadata = {\n            \'page_count\': len(artifact.content.split(\'\\n\\n\')),\n            \'word_count\': len(artifact.content.split()),\n            \'format\': \'markdown-to-pdf\'\n        }\n        artifact.file_path = f"/workspace/artifacts/{artifact.id}.pdf"\n        artifact.file_size = len(artifact.content.encode(\'utf-8\'))\n        \n        return artifact\n        \n    async def validate(self, artifact: Artifact) -> Dict:\n        """Validate PDF artifact"""\n        results = {\n            \'valid\': True,\n            \'issues\': [],\n            \'score\': 0.0\n        }\n        \n        # Check content exists\n        if not artifact.content or len(artifact.content) < 100:\n            results[\'valid\'] = False\n            results[\'issues\'].append("Content too short or missing")\n            results[\'score\'] = 0.3\n        else:\n            results[\'score\'] = 0.9\n            \n        # Check structure\n        if \'##\' not in artifact.content:\n            results[\'issues\'].append("Missing section headers")\n            results[\'score\'] -= 0.1\n            \n        return results\n\nclass DOCXGenerator(ArtifactGenerator):\n    """Generates DOCX documents"""\n    \n    async def generate(self, document: Dict, prompts: List[str], swarm_results: List[Dict]) -> Artifact:\n        """Generate DOCX from document"""\n        artifact = Artifact(ArtifactType.DOCX, f"{document[\'title\']}.docx", document[\'id\'])\n        artifact.status = ArtifactStatus.GENERATING\n        \n        if self.llm_router:\n            content_prompt = f"""Generate a professional Word document with the following:\nTitle: {document[\'title\']}\nContent: {document[\'content\']}\n\nInclude:\n- Title page\n- Table of contents\n- Multiple sections with headings\n- Bullet points and numbered lists\n- Professional formatting\n\nFormat as structured text."""\n            \n            response = await self.llm_router.generate(content_prompt, temperature=0.3)\n            artifact.content = response.get(\'content\', \'\')\n        else:\n            artifact.content = f"""TITLE PAGE\n{document[\'title\']}\n\nTABLE OF CONTENTS\n1. Introduction\n2. Main Content\n3. Analysis\n4. Conclusions\n\nSECTION 1: INTRODUCTION\n{document[\'content\'][:300]}\n\nSECTION 2: MAIN CONTENT\n{document[\'content\']}\n\nSECTION 3: ANALYSIS\nThis section provides detailed analysis of the content.\n\nSECTION 4: CONCLUSIONS\nSummary and final thoughts.\n"""\n        \n        artifact.status = ArtifactStatus.VALIDATING\n        artifact.metadata = {\n            \'sections\': 4,\n            \'word_count\': len(artifact.content.split()),\n            \'format\': \'docx\'\n        }\n        artifact.file_path = f"/workspace/artifacts/{artifact.id}.docx"\n        artifact.file_size = len(artifact.content.encode(\'utf-8\'))\n        \n        return artifact\n        \n    async def validate(self, artifact: Artifact) -> Dict:\n        """Validate DOCX artifact"""\n        results = {\n            \'valid\': True,\n            \'issues\': [],\n            \'score\': 0.85\n        }\n        \n        if not artifact.content or len(artifact.content) < 200:\n            results[\'valid\'] = False\n            results[\'issues\'].append("Content insufficient")\n            results[\'score\'] = 0.4\n            \n        return results\n\nclass CodeGenerator(ArtifactGenerator):\n    """Generates code artifacts"""\n    \n    async def generate(self, document: Dict, prompts: List[str], swarm_results: List[Dict]) -> Artifact:\n        """Generate code from document"""\n        artifact = Artifact(ArtifactType.CODE, f"{document[\'title\']}.py", document[\'id\'])\n        artifact.status = ArtifactStatus.GENERATING\n        \n        if self.llm_router:\n            code_prompt = f"""Generate production-ready Python code based on:\nTitle: {document[\'title\']}\nRequirements: {document[\'content\']}\n\nInclude:\n- Proper imports\n- Class definitions\n- Function implementations\n- Error handling\n- Documentation strings\n- Type hints\n- Unit tests\n\nGenerate complete, runnable code."""\n            \n            response = await self.llm_router.generate(code_prompt, temperature=0.2)\n            artifact.content = response.get(\'content\', \'\')\n        else:\n            artifact.content = f\'\'\'"""\n{document[\'title\']}\nGenerated from Living Document\n"""\n\nfrom typing import Dict, List, Optional\nimport logging\n\nlogger = logging.getLogger(__name__)\n\nclass GeneratedSystem:\n    """Main system class"""\n    \n    def __init__(self):\n        self.initialized = False\n        logger.info("System initialized")\n        \n    def process(self, data: Dict) -> Dict:\n        """Process data"""\n        try:\n            result = {{"status": "success", "data": data}}\n            return result\n        except Exception as e:\n            logger.error(f"Processing error: {{e}}")\n            return {{"status": "error", "message": str(e)}}\n            \n    def validate(self, data: Dict) -> bool:\n        """Validate data"""\n        return bool(data)\n\nif __name__ == "__main__":\n    system = GeneratedSystem()\n    print("System ready")\n\'\'\'\n        \n        artifact.status = ArtifactStatus.VALIDATING\n        artifact.metadata = {\n            \'language\': \'python\',\n            \'lines\': len(artifact.content.split(\'\\n\')),\n            \'has_tests\': \'test_\' in artifact.content.lower()\n        }\n        artifact.file_path = f"/workspace/artifacts/{artifact.id}.py"\n        artifact.file_size = len(artifact.content.encode(\'utf-8\'))\n        \n        return artifact\n        \n    async def validate(self, artifact: Artifact) -> Dict:\n        """Validate code artifact"""\n        results = {\n            \'valid\': True,\n            \'issues\': [],\n            \'score\': 0.0\n        }\n        \n        # Check for basic code structure\n        if \'def \' not in artifact.content and \'class \' not in artifact.content:\n            results[\'valid\'] = False\n            results[\'issues\'].append("No functions or classes found")\n            results[\'score\'] = 0.3\n        else:\n            results[\'score\'] = 0.85\n            \n        # Check for imports\n        if \'import \' not in artifact.content:\n            results[\'issues\'].append("No imports found")\n            results[\'score\'] -= 0.1\n            \n        return results\n\nclass Artifact:\n        """Generate design artifact"""\n        artifact = Artifact(ArtifactType.DESIGN, f"{document[\'title\']}_design.svg", document[\'id\'])\n        artifact.status = Update allowed fields\n        if \'name\' in updates:\n            artifact.name = updates[\'name\']\n        if \'content\' in updates:\n            artifact.content = updates[\'content\']\n            self._save_to_file(artifact)\n        if \'metadata\' in updates:\n            artifact.metadata.update(updates[\'metadata\'])\n        if \'status\' in updates:\n            try:\n                artifact.status = ArtifactStatus(updates[\'status\'])\n            except ValueError:\n                pass\n                \n        artifact.updated_at = datetime.now().isoformat()\n        \n        return artifact\n        \n    def delete_artifact(self, artifact_id: str) -> bool:\n        """Delete an artifact"""\n        artifact = self.artifacts.get(artifact_id)\n        if not artifact:\n            return False\n            \n        # Delete file if it exists\n        if artifact.file_path and os.path.exists(artifact.file_path):\n            try:\n                os.remove(artifact.file_path)\n            except:\n                pass\n                \n        # Remove from memory\n        del self.artifacts[artifact_id]\n        if artifact_id in self.version_history:\n            del self.version_history[artifact_id]\n            \n        return True\n        \n    def create_version(self, artifact_id: str, content: str, \n                      metadata: Optional[Dict] = None) -> Optional[Artifact]:\n        """Create a new version of an artifact"""\n        artifact = self.artifacts.get(artifact_id)\n        if not artifact:\n            return None\n            \n        # Increment version\n        artifact.version += 1\n        artifact.content = content\n        artifact.updated_at = datetime.now().isoformat()\n        \n        if metadata:\n            artifact.metadata.update(metadata)\n            \n        # Save to version history\n        self.version_history[artifact_id].append({\n            \'version\': artifact.version,\n            \'created_at\': artifact.updated_at,\n            \'quality_score\': artifact.quality_score,\n            \'status\': artifact.status.value,\n            \'metadata\': artifact.metadata.copy()\n        })\n        \n        # Restore metadata from target version\n        artifact.metadata = target_version[\'metadata\'].copy()\n        artifact.quality_score = target_version[\'quality_score\']\n        artifact.status = ArtifactStatus(target_version[\'status\'])\n        artifact.updated_at = datetime.now().isoformat()\n        \n        return artifact\n        \n    def convert_format(self, artifact_id: str, target_format: str) -> Optional[Artifact]:\n        """Convert artifact to a different format"""\n        artifact = self.artifacts.get(artifact_id)\n        if not artifact:\n            return None\n            \n        # Create a new artifact with converted format\n        from artifact_generation_system import Artifact as NewArtifact\n        \n        converted = NewArtifact(\n            ArtifactType(target_format),\n            f"{artifact.name}_converted",\n            artifact.source_doc_id\n        )\n        \n        # Copy content and metadata\n        converted.content = artifact.content\n        converted.metadata = artifact.metadata.copy()\n        converted.metadata[\'converted_from\'] = artifact.type.value\n        converted.metadata[\'original_id\'] = artifact.id\n        converted.quality_score = artifact.quality_score * 0.9  # Search in name\n            if query_lower in artifact.name.lower():\n                results.append(artifact.to_dict())\n                continue\n                \n            # Search in content\n            if artifact.content and query_lower in artifact.content.lower():\n                results.append(artifact.to_dict())\n                continue\n                \n            # Count by type\n            type_key = artifact.type.value\n            stats[\'by_type\'][type_key] = stats[\'by_type\'].get(type_key, 0) + 1\n            \n            # Count by status\n            status_key = artifact.status.value\n            stats[\'by_status\'][status_key] = stats[\'by_status\'].get(status_key, 0) + 1\n            \n            # Sum file sizes\n            stats[\'total_size\'] += artifact.file_size\n            \n            # Sum quality scores\n            quality_sum += artifact.quality_score\n            \n        # Calculate average quality\n        if len(self.artifacts) > 0:\n            stats[\'average_quality\'] = quality_sum / len(self.artifacts)\n            \n        return stats\n        \n    def _save_to_file(self, artifact: Artifact) -> bool:\n        """Save artifact content to file"""\n        if not artifact.content or not artifact.file_path:\n            return False\n            \n        try:\n            # Ensure directory exists\n            os.makedirs(os.path.dirname(artifact.file_path), exist_ok=True)\n            \n            # Write content to file\n            with open(artifact.file_path, \'w\', encoding=\'utf-8\') as f:\n                f.write(artifact.content)\n                \n            # Update file size\n            artifact.file_size = os.path.getsize(artifact.file_path)\n            \n            return True\n        except Exception as e:\n            print(f"Error saving artifact to file: {e}")\n            return False\n            \n    def _load_from_file(self, artifact: Artifact) -> bool:\n        """Load artifact content from file"""\n        if not artifact.file_path or not os.path.exists(artifact.file_path):\n            return False\n            \n        try:\n            with open(artifact.file_path, \'r\', encoding=\'utf-8\') as f:\n                artifact.content = f.read()\n            return True\n        except Exception as e:\n            print(f"Error loading artifact from file: {e}")\n            return False\n            \n    def export_artifact(self, artifact_id: str, export_path: str) -> bool:\n        """Export artifact to a specific path"""\n        artifact = self.artifacts.get(artifact_id)\n        if not artifact or not artifact.content:\n            return False\n            \n        try:\n            # Ensure export directory exists\n            os.makedirs(os.path.dirname(export_path), exist_ok=True)\n            \n            # Write to export path\n            with open(export_path, \'w\', encoding=\'utf-8\') as f:\n                f.write(artifact.content)\n                \n            return True\n        except Exception as e:\n            print(f"Error exporting artifact: {e}")\n            return False\n            \n    def import_artifact(self, file_path: str, artifact_type: str, \n                       name: str, source_doc_id: str) -> Optional[Artifact]:\n        """Import an artifact from a file"""\n        if not os.path.exists(file_path):\n            return None\n            \n        try:\n            # Sort by version descending\n        history.sort(key=lambda x: x[\'version\'], reverse=True)\n        \n        # Keep only the most recent versions\n        self.version_history[artifact_id] = history[:keep_versions]\n        \n        # Let me create the backend components:\n\n<function_calls>\n<create-file file_path="shadow_agent_system.py">\n"""\nShadow Agent Learning System\nObserves user actions, learns patterns, and proposes automations\n"""\n\nimport json\nimport uuid\nfrom datetime import datetime, timedelta\nfrom typing import Dict, List, Optional, Any\nfrom collections import defaultdict\nfrom enum import Enum\n\nclass ObservationType(Enum):\n    """Types of observations"""\n    COMMAND = "command"\n    STATE_CHANGE = "state_change"\n    ARTIFACT_GENERATION = "artifact_generation"\n    DOCUMENT_EDIT = "document_edit"\n    APPROVAL = "approval"\n    REJECTION = "rejection"\n\nclass ProposalStatus(Enum):\n    """Status of automation proposals"""\n    PENDING = "pending"\n    APPROVED = "approved"\n    REJECTED = "rejected"\n    ACTIVE = "active"\n    PAUSED = "paused"\n\nclass AutomationTrigger(Enum):\n    """Types of automation triggers"""\n    TIME_BASED = "time_based"\n    EVENT_BASED = "event_based"\n    PATTERN_BASED = "pattern_based"\n    THRESHOLD_BASED = "threshold_based"\n\nclass Observation:\n    """Represents a single observed action"""\n    \n    def __init__(self, obs_type: ObservationType, action: str, context: Dict):\n        self.id = str(uuid.uuid4())\n        self.type = obs_type\n        self.action = action\n        self.context = context\n        self.timestamp = datetime.now().isoformat()\n        self.user_id = context.get(\'user_id\', \'default\')\n        self.session_id = context.get(\'session_id\', \'default\')\n        \n    def to_dict(self) -> Dict:\n        """Convert observation to dictionary"""\n        return {\n            \'id\': self.id,\n            \'type\': self.type.value,\n            \'action\': self.action,\n            \'context\': self.context,\n            \'timestamp\': self.timestamp,\n            \'user_id\': self.user_id,\n            \'session_id\': self.session_id\n        }\n\nclass Pattern:\n    """Represents a detected pattern in user behavior"""\n    \n    def __init__(self, pattern_type: str, description: str, observations: List[Observation]):\n        self.id = str(uuid.uuid4())\n        self.type = pattern_type\n        self.description = description\n        self.observations = observations\n        self.frequency = len(observations)\n        self.confidence = 0.0\n        self.first_seen = observations[0].timestamp if observations else datetime.now().isoformat()\n        self.last_seen = observations[-1].timestamp if observations else datetime.now().isoformat()\n        self.detected_at = datetime.now().isoformat()\n        \n    def calculate_confidence(self):\n        """Calculate confidence score based on frequency and consistency"""\n        # Base confidence on frequency\n        if self.frequency < 3:\n            self.confidence = 0.3\n        elif self.frequency < 5:\n            self.confidence = 0.5\n        elif self.frequency < 10:\n            self.confidence = 0.7\n        else:\n            self.confidence = 0.9\n            \n        # Adjust for time consistency\n        if len(self.observations) >= 2:\n            timestamps = [datetime.fromisoformat(obs.timestamp) for obs in self.observations]\n            time_diffs = [(timestamps[i+1] - timestamps[i]).total_seconds() \n                         for i in range(len(timestamps)-1)]\n            \n            if time_diffs:\n                avg_diff = sum(time_diffs) / len(time_diffs)\n                std_dev = (sum((x - avg_diff) ** 2 for x in time_diffs) / len(time_diffs)) ** 0.5\n                \n                # More consistent timing = higher confidence\n                if std_dev < avg_diff * 0.2:  # Very consistent\n                    self.confidence = min(1.0, self.confidence + 0.1)\n                    \n    def to_dict(self) -> Dict:\n        """Convert pattern to dictionary"""\n        return {\n            \'id\': self.id,\n            \'type\': self.type,\n            \'description\': self.description,\n            \'frequency\': self.frequency,\n            \'confidence\': self.confidence,\n            \'first_seen\': self.first_seen,\n            \'last_seen\': self.last_seen,\n            \'detected_at\': self.detected_at,\n            \'observation_count\': len(self.observations)\n        }\n\nclass AutomationProposal:\n    """Represents a proposed automation"""\n    \n    def __init__(self, pattern: Pattern, automation_type: str, description: str):\n        self.id = str(uuid.uuid4())\n        self.pattern_id = pattern.id\n        self.type = automation_type\n        self.description = description\n        self.trigger = AutomationTrigger.PATTERN_BASED\n        self.status = ProposalStatus.PENDING\n        self.confidence = pattern.confidence\n        self.created_at = datetime.now().isoformat()\n        self.approved_at = None\n        self.rejected_at = None\n        self.rejection_reason = None\n        self.execution_count = 0\n        self.success_count = 0\n        self.failure_count = 0\n        self.last_executed = None\n        self.actions = []\n        self.conditions = []\n        \n    def approve(self):\n        """Approve the proposal"""\n        self.status = ProposalStatus.APPROVED\n        self.approved_at = datetime.now().isoformat()\n        \n    def reject(self, reason: str = None):\n        """Reject the proposal"""\n        self.status = ProposalStatus.REJECTED\n        self.rejected_at = datetime.now().isoformat()\n        self.rejection_reason = reason\n        \n    def activate(self):\n        """Activate the automation"""\n        if self.status == ProposalStatus.APPROVED:\n            self.status = ProposalStatus.ACTIVE\n            \n    def pause(self):\n        """Pause the automation"""\n        if self.status == ProposalStatus.ACTIVE:\n            self.status = ProposalStatus.PAUSED\n            \n    def record_execution(self, success: bool):\n        """Record an execution result"""\n        self.execution_count += 1\n        if success:\n            self.success_count += 1\n        else:\n            self.failure_count += 1\n        self.last_executed = datetime.now().isoformat()\n        \n        # Update confidence based on success rate\n        if self.execution_count > 0:\n            success_rate = self.success_count / self.execution_count\n            self.confidence = (self.confidence + success_rate) / 2\n            \n    def to_dict(self) -> Dict:\n        """Convert proposal to dictionary"""\n        return {\n            \'id\': self.id,\n            \'pattern_id\': self.pattern_id,\n            \'type\': self.type,\n            \'description\': self.description,\n            \'trigger\': self.trigger.value,\n            \'status\': self.status.value,\n            \'confidence\': self.confidence,\n            \'created_at\': self.created_at,\n            \'approved_at\': self.approved_at,\n            \'rejected_at\': self.rejected_at,\n            \'rejection_reason\': self.rejection_reason,\n            \'execution_count\': self.execution_count,\n            \'success_count\': self.success_count,\n            \'failure_count\': self.failure_count,\n            \'last_executed\': self.last_executed,\n            \'actions\': self.actions,\n            \'conditions\': self.conditions\n        }\n\nclass ShadowAgent:\n    """A shadow agent that observes and learns"""\n    \n    def __init__(self, name: str, domain: str):\n        self.id = str(uuid.uuid4())\n        self.name = name\n        self.domain = domain\n        self.observations = []\n        self.patterns = []\n        self.proposals = []\n        self.active_automations = []\n        self.learning_enabled = True\n        self.created_at = datetime.now().isoformat()\n        self.last_learning_cycle = None\n        self.total_observations = 0\n        self.total_patterns = 0\n        self.total_proposals = 0\n        \n    def observe(self, obs_type: ObservationType, action: str, context: Dict):\n        """Record an observation"""\n        if not self.learning_enabled:\n            return\n            \n        observation = Observation(obs_type, action, context)\n        self.observations.append(observation)\n        self.total_observations += 1\n        \n        # Limit observation history\n        if len(self.observations) > 1000:\n            self.observations = self.observations[-1000:]\n            \n    def analyze_patterns(self) -> List[Pattern]:\n        """Analyze observations to detect patterns"""\n        if len(self.observations) < 3:\n            return []\n            \n        detected_patterns = []\n        \n        # Pattern 1: Repeated commands\n        command_sequences = defaultdict(list)\n        for obs in self.observations:\n            if obs.type == ObservationType.COMMAND:\n                command_sequences[obs.action].append(obs)\n                \n        for action, obs_list in command_sequences.items():\n            if len(obs_list) >= 3:\n                pattern = Pattern(\n                    "repeated_command",\n                    f"User frequently executes: {action}",\n                    obs_list\n                )\n                pattern.calculate_confidence()\n                detected_patterns.append(pattern)\n                \n        # Pattern 2: Command sequences\n        if len(self.observations) >= 5:\n            for i in range(len(self.observations) - 2):\n                seq = [self.observations[i], self.observations[i+1], self.observations[i+2]]\n                if all(obs.type == ObservationType.COMMAND for obs in seq):\n                    seq_str = " → ".join([obs.action for obs in seq])\n                    \n                    # Check if this sequence appears multiple times\n                    count = 0\n                    for j in range(len(self.observations) - 2):\n                        check_seq = [self.observations[j], self.observations[j+1], self.observations[j+2]]\n                        check_str = " → ".join([obs.action for obs in check_seq])\n                        if check_str == seq_str:\n                            count += 1\n                            \n                    if count >= 2:\n                        pattern = Pattern(\n                            "command_sequence",\n                            f"User often executes sequence: {seq_str}",\n                            seq\n                        )\n                        pattern.frequency = count\n                        pattern.calculate_confidence()\n                        detected_patterns.append(pattern)\n                        break  # Only detect first sequence\n                        \n        # Pattern 3: Time-based patterns\n        time_based = defaultdict(list)\n        for obs in self.observations:\n            hour = datetime.fromisoformat(obs.timestamp).hour\n            time_based[hour].append(obs)\n            \n        for hour, obs_list in time_based.items():\n            if len(obs_list) >= 5:\n                pattern = Pattern(\n                    "time_based",\n                    f"User is active around {hour}:00",\n                    obs_list\n                )\n                pattern.calculate_confidence()\n                detected_patterns.append(pattern)\n                \n        # Pattern 4: Artifact generation patterns\n        artifact_types = defaultdict(list)\n        for obs in self.observations:\n            if obs.type == ObservationType.ARTIFACT_GENERATION:\n                artifact_type = obs.context.get(\'artifact_type\', \'unknown\')\n                artifact_types[artifact_type].append(obs)\n                \n        for art_type, obs_list in artifact_types.items():\n            if len(obs_list) >= 3:\n                pattern = Pattern(\n                    "artifact_preference",\n                    f"User frequently generates {art_type} artifacts",\n                    obs_list\n                )\n                pattern.calculate_confidence()\n                detected_patterns.append(pattern)\n                \n        self.patterns.extend(detected_patterns)\n        self.total_patterns += len(detected_patterns)\n        self.last_learning_cycle = datetime.now().isoformat()\n        \n        return detected_patterns\n        \n    def generate_proposals(self, patterns: List[Pattern]) -> List[AutomationProposal]:\n        """Generate automation proposals from patterns"""\n        new_proposals = []\n        \n        for pattern in patterns:\n            if pattern.confidence < 0.5:\n                continue  # Only propose high-confidence patterns\n                \n            proposal = None\n            \n            if pattern.type == "repeated_command":\n                proposal = AutomationProposal(\n                    pattern,\n                    "command_automation",\n                    f"Automate: {pattern.description}"\n                )\n                proposal.actions = [{\'type\': \'execute_command\', \'command\': pattern.observations[0].action}]\n                proposal.trigger = AutomationTrigger.EVENT_BASED\n                \n            elif pattern.type == "command_sequence":\n                proposal = AutomationProposal(\n                    pattern,\n                    "sequence_automation",\n                    f"Automate sequence: {pattern.description}"\n                )\n                proposal.actions = [\n                    {\'type\': \'execute_command\', \'command\': obs.action}\n                    for obs in pattern.observations[:3]\n                ]\n                proposal.trigger = AutomationTrigger.PATTERN_BASED\n                \n            elif pattern.type == "time_based":\n                proposal = AutomationProposal(\n                    pattern,\n                    "scheduled_automation",\n                    f"Schedule tasks: {pattern.description}"\n                )\n                proposal.trigger = AutomationTrigger.TIME_BASED\n                \n            elif pattern.type == "artifact_preference":\n                proposal = AutomationProposal(\n                    pattern,\n                    "artifact_automation",\n                    f"Auto-generate artifacts: {pattern.description}"\n                )\n                proposal.trigger = AutomationTrigger.EVENT_BASED\n                \n            if proposal:\n                self.proposals.append(proposal)\n                new_proposals.append(proposal)\n                self.total_proposals += 1\n                \n        return new_proposals\n        \n    def to_dict(self) -> Dict:\n        """Convert shadow agent to dictionary"""\n        return {\n            \'id\': self.id,\n            \'name\': self.name,\n            \'domain\': self.domain,\n            \'learning_enabled\': self.learning_enabled,\n            \'created_at\': self.created_at,\n            \'last_learning_cycle\': self.last_learning_cycle,\n            \'total_observations\': self.total_observations,\n            \'total_patterns\': self.total_patterns,\n            \'total_proposals\': self.total_proposals,\n            \'recent_observations\': len(self.observations),\n            \'active_automations\': len(self.active_automations)\n        }\n\nclass ShadowAgentSystem:\n    """Main system for managing shadow agents"""\n    \n    def __init__(self):\n        self.agents: Dict[str, ShadowAgent] = {}\n        self.global_observations = []\n        self.global_patterns = []\n        self.global_proposals = []\n        \n        # Create default shadow agents\n        self._create_default_agents()\n        \n    def _create_default_agents(self):\n        """Create default shadow agents for each domain"""\n        domains = [\n            ("Command Observer", "command_system"),\n            ("Document Watcher", "living_documents"),\n            ("Artifact Monitor", "artifact_generation"),\n            ("State Tracker", "state_machine"),\n            ("Workflow Analyzer", "workflows")\n        ]\n        \n        for name, domain in domains:\n            agent = ShadowAgent(name, domain)\n            self.agents[agent.id] = agent\n            \n    def get_agent(self, agent_id: str) -> Optional[ShadowAgent]:\n        """Get shadow agent by ID"""\n        return self.agents.get(agent_id)\n        \n    def list_agents(self) -> List[Dict]:\n        """List all shadow agents"""\n        return [agent.to_dict() for agent in self.agents.values()]\n        \n    def observe(self, domain: str, obs_type: ObservationType, action: str, context: Dict):\n        """Record observation across relevant agents"""\n        self.global_observations.append({\n            \'domain\': domain,\n            \'type\': obs_type.value,\n            \'action\': action,\n            \'context\': context,\n            \'timestamp\': datetime.now().isoformat()\n        })\n        \n        # Distribute to relevant agents\n        for agent in self.agents.values():\n            if agent.domain == domain or agent.domain == "workflows":\n                agent.observe(obs_type, action, context)\n                \n    def run_learning_cycle(self) -> Dict:\n        """Run learning cycle across all agents"""\n        results = {\n            \'agents_analyzed\': 0,\n            \'patterns_detected\': 0,\n            \'proposals_generated\': 0,\n            \'timestamp\': datetime.now().isoformat()\n        }\n        \n        for agent in self.agents.values():\n            if not agent.learning_enabled:\n                continue\n                \n            # Analyze patterns\n            patterns = agent.analyze_patterns()\n            results[\'patterns_detected\'] += len(patterns)\n            \n
